CREATE TABLE sensors (
    sensor_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    sensor_type VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    location VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    city_id INT,
    FOREIGN KEY (city_id) REFERENCES city(city_id)
);

    event_date DATE,
